if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '78594253acc6b5c354e6e8c5226170c785d85356') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '78594253acc6b5c354e6e8c5226170c785d85356') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '732494ef690784b88f7704f552c06c4ec6b28bf9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '78594253acc6b5c354e6e8c5226170c785d85356') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != 'd57d31666342d4554a1eb9a28d3ee5e05ab14f80') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'd57d31666342d4554a1eb9a28d3ee5e05ab14f80') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '599768801b6a963780d28710084a402ac598ea28') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'd57d31666342d4554a1eb9a28d3ee5e05ab14f80') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js') != 'dae012fb0b14b15ef4518d7c54234982f60a3835') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js') !== 'dae012fb0b14b15ef4518d7c54234982f60a3835') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js') !== '1c612043ba173a701a61b60c0394d5db10894a28') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js') !== 'dae012fb0b14b15ef4518d7c54234982f60a3835') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/emn178/js-sha3/build/sha3.min.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/licenses');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/licenses');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/licenses') != '83cf6df055b74a117ccbca60ee7a4f9d517eea5c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/licenses', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/licenses');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '83cf6df055b74a117ccbca60ee7a4f9d517eea5c') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '3a06a899e728c0c1608cb2dbf5e87b6e8f3d29f3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/licenses');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/licenses');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/licenses')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/licenses', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '83cf6df055b74a117ccbca60ee7a4f9d517eea5c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1395\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1395') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
